## This Week in Security: Your News Briefing

Welcome to your weekly security roundup. We've tracked down the **10 most important stories** this
week‚Äîthe ones everyone's talking about, from critical threats to emerging trends that could shape
your security posture. Leading the news this week is **Appsec Roundup - June 2025**, which has
sparked conversation across 9 sources. Meanwhile, the industry is closely tracking **Secure By
Design roundup - Dec/Jan 2026** with 6 mentions, along with emerging details on **CVE-2019-25376 |
OPNsense 19.1 Proxy Endpoint ignoreLogACL cross...**, **CVE-2026-2530 | Wavlink WL-WN579A3 up to
20210219...**, and **CVE-2025-9961**. Here's the full breakdown of what you need to know.

### üö® Critical Threats This Week

First, the stories that demand your immediate attention:

**1. Appsec Roundup - June 2025**
   Mentioned across 9 industry sources this week. Lots of fascinating threat model-related advances, new risk management tools, games, and more!.
   [Get the details ‚Üí](https://shostack.org/blog/appsec-roundup-june-2025/)

**2. Secure By Design roundup - Dec/Jan 2026**
   Mentioned across 6 industry sources this week. The normalization of deviance, exciting threat modeling news, and a question of do regulatory threats change ‚Äòthe threat.
   [Get the details ‚Üí](https://shostack.org/blog/appsec-roundup-dec-jan-2026/)

**3. CVE-2019-25376 | OPNsense 19.1 Proxy Endpoint ignoreLogACL cross site scripting (Exploit 46351 / EDB-46351)**
   Mentioned across 6 industry sources this week. A vulnerability classified as problematic has been found in OPNsense 19.
   [Get the details ‚Üí](https://nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2019-25376)

### üõ†Ô∏è Tools, Updates & Releases

New capabilities and releases worth knowing about:

**1. Promoting AI Security ‚Äî Acting Assistant Privacy Commissioner Speaks at the GenA.I. Symposium**
   . Referenced in 2 stories this week.
   [Explore ‚Üí](http://www.pcpd.org.hk/english/whatsnew/20251031.html)

### What You Should Do Next

**Monitor these** in your environment next week:
- Any new CVE announcements related to systems you operate
- Emerging attack techniques being discussed in the community
- Updates and patches for tools your team uses

**Have a look at** the full deep-dives in the trending stories below. Each one provides context that could inform your security decisions this week.

## Cyber Regulatory

<details class="group border-b border-border/50 py-1">

## Threat Intel & Vulnerability

<details class="group border-b border-border/50 py-1">
  <summary class="cursor-pointer hover:bg-secondary/30 transition-colors list-none flex items-center justify-between py-1.5 px-2">
    <div class="flex-1 flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center gap-1 md:gap-3 overflow-hidden mr-4">
      <span class="text-sm font-medium text-foreground whitespace-nowrap overflow-hidden text-ellipsis md:max-w-[50%]">CVE-2025-70795</span>
      <span class="text-xs text-muted-foreground whitespace-nowrap overflow-hidden text-ellipsis flex-1">Currently trending CVE - Hype Score: 20</span>
    </div>
    <span class="text-muted-foreground text-xs shrink-0 group-open:rotate-180 transition-transform">‚ñº</span>
  </summary>
